            <h3 class="entry-title td-module-title"><a href="https://www.altcoinbuzz.io/product-release/coingate-added-support-for-litecoin-lightning-network-payments/"  rel="bookmark" title="CoinGate Added Support for Litecoin Lightning Network Payments">CoinGate Added Support for Litecoin Lightning Network Payments</a></h3>
            <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name"><a href="https://www.altcoinbuzz.io/author/victor/">Victor</a> <span>-</span> </span>                <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2019-02-11T02:31:18+08:00" >February 11, 2019</time></span>                <span class="td-module-comments"><a href="https://www.altcoinbuzz.io/product-release/coingate-added-support-for-litecoin-lightning-network-payments/#respond">0</a></span>            </div>

            <div class="td-excerpt">
                CoinGate announced that it has added support for Litecoin (LTC) Lightning Network payments, enabling faster payments with lower fees.
Lithuania-based CoinGate, a payment gateway for blockchain payments, announced in...            </div>
